You can disable this feature in the settings page \"Synchronize map with compass (when follow or play is unactive)\". If the option is checked the map rotate with you, otherwise the map is always facing north.\r\n\r\n2) Follow me and draw route on the map. This way, if you go from point A to point B, you can record the route.\r\n\r\n3) Follow me and don't draw route on the map. In the menu you must click on \"Start follow me / Stop follow me\".
